<username>Dennis Obtera< /username><time>1580960858179<//time><Rating>5<//Rating>< review>
I've been living here at eaves Rancho Pensasquitos for about a year now. Since my stay, I have nothing but good things to say about this place.

Review of the Staff:
When first applying for the apartment, Andrea and Sophia took great care of me. They were informative during the the whole process while maintaining their professionalism and kindness. It didn't stop there. Throughout my stay, the staff constantly helped me with any situation that arose, and always made me feel at home.

My washer and dryer combo stopped working (2) times throughout the stay here. Sure enough , as I put a support ticket on through their website, John came over the next day or same day and fixed it. I always see John around the complex and even stop to have conversations with him.  He is always a pleasure to talk to with a smile on his face.

There were a few other items that ended up needing attention.  I opened up my garage and it seems a pipe burst. Andrea was quick to react, and made sure I was happy with the results on how she remedied the situation.  Whenever I see Andrea around the complex, I am always greeted with a hello and the extra reassurance making sure I was happy here.  She even remembers items I've brought up in the past to make sure everything is still ok.

Upon lease renewal, I did not hesitate one bit to renew.  With Andrea and John around, I am not surprised many residents stay for years.

Review of the Complex:
I've lived at a few different complexes and this one is probably my favorite.

1.  Parking - I have a garage and can fit my car , lifted truck, tools, and a few spare parts. Additionally, there are plenty of spots on the street so parking is never really an issue. This was one of the biggest problems I've experienced at most places, but not here.

2.  Living space - Pretty standard set up for this price range. It's nothing fancy, but definitely not cheap. Everything was in good shape and clean when moving in.  No complaints here.

3.  Overall Community - Everyone is respectful and greets each other (I even made a few friends). The complex is always maintained and kept clean.

5 Stars< /review>

I wish I could share our entire story regarding this location, but it would be a bit too long of a read.
From the moment I was given a tour of this community, I recognized it was different from others. The staff were very welcoming and were genuinely friendly people. *Update*

<review>Updated Review as of Ocotber 2019:

5 stars

My initial review wasn't based on customer service, residential environment, or any related issues. It was solely based on regional management and their disruptive management. Enough of that, let's get to the actual review.

Eaves Rancho Penasquitos is located 20 minutes from Fashion Valley, La Jolla, and the North County mall, and is literally minutes from the 15 and the 56 Freeway. The residence and environment is quiet and peaceful. They are pet friendly. After speaking to many of the residents, despite being pet friendly, they have never heard a dog bark unrelentingly or have seen dog poop in the common areas. The property is well-maintained and has the amenities that anyone would want, you can read them for yourself on their website. If you are looking for an apartment that is centrally located and I believe is competitively priced, you may want to consider giving them a call.

Currently, the local staff at the residence and the new manager are incredible. Great skills, very friendly, and always willing to solve issues that come up. Despite the fact that it is not easy to solve each and everyone's problems and concerns, they always make an attempt to provide solutions, and I think that is awesome. Hopefully the current staff that theybhs e will stay in place for a while, instead of being yanked and sent elsewhere.

In closing, I just want to give a shoutout to both Tasha and Sophia in the office, as well as John in Maintenance, and one of the ladies who don't really go unnoticed, I don't know her name, she is super quiet, she always makes it a point to keep the property clean.

--

My fianc√© and I have lived in a handful of apartments in San Diego, Eaves at Rancho Penasquitos has been the most pleasant experience!

<Date>1518373210729< /Date><Rating>5< /Rating>< text>
The service here is awesome! The owner/chef and woman that cashiers are extremely nice. I don't frequent too much and they remember who I am. That says a lot. The prices are also super affordable.

Here's a tip next time you visit. If you order from the outside window, peek in and watch the chef make your order. He's so organized, clean, and professional. He's got one hand grilling and one hand cleaning his food area. Makes the food taste that much better from what it already is.

The burgers are so good. Tastes the same every time with the right amount of everything. And their fries are delicious! Crispy and that seasoning puts them over other places. Enjoy!<//text>

< review>
I have had a noise coming from the rear left tire on my car for the past 3.5 yrs and have been multiple places to get it fixed. None were able to do so and I was left with an annoyingly loud squeak as I'd drive down the road.

After reading the reviews, I decided to visit Antonio's to see if Fred could get the job done.

Once I arrived, Fred was eager to hear my problems and put my car on the rack immediately. He asked me to stand right there with him while he worked on my car and explained everything he was doing. Within 30 mins, he had disassembled the entire rear assembly to check everything. He determined that the edges of the brake pads were the issue and did a quick grind on them. After putting the car back together, Fred sent me on a test drive and the noise was no more. When I asked for my bill, he said that there was no charge since he didn't make any major changes or additions to fix the problem.

I got several of his business cards and intend to send all of my friends to him. I can't say enough about how nice it was to work with an honest, knowledgeable tech when having my car repaired.<//review>

< Text>
I came to Antonio's Auto Care to get my vehicle smog tested as requested by the DMV. Fred and his Associates were very professional and hard working individuals.

They began working on the smog test immediately and went through with great speed and ease. Within a very short and reasonable amount of time I had my smog test completed.

My vehicle was unable to pass the entire smog test (Due to the fact that I had replaced the battery just the day before.) And Fred was very helpful in offering his advice and expertise to what needed to be done for me to fix the problem. He told me to drive the car around and come back, and he would check to see if it was ready to be smog checked.

I followed his advice and drove around for a bit, and he checked the computer of the car to see if it was ready, and informed me it wasn't. He did this free of charge! He was even able to show me the device showing what he was looking for, and suggested that I try driving at least 100 more miles.

After having done 100 miles, he checked the computer of the car one last time (Free of charge!) and found that finally the vehicle was completely ready for the smog test. And within a very short amount of time the smog test was completed and the car passed.

A very nice shop with the latest equipment, and all of the workers are hard working people. I also learned that the shop and its associates are ASE certified. Very friendly and hard working group of people, I would recommend to anyone! Plus they are Trilingual!< /Text>

< Text>
Drove over a road dip at Pomerado & Rios which broke the oil pan. Saturday morning I noticed a lot of oil in the carport. I had an 8:30am meeting in Poway but then chose to stop by an auto shop beforehand to get an opinion and a solution. I arrived at Antonio's Autocare at 7:55am at the same time as Matthew and Fred. No sooner had I parked and began relating the problem that Matthew was under the car saying what I suspected: the oil pan needed replacement. Matthew took a picture of the damaged pan with his cellphone to show me the white strips of concrete that had caused the damage.
Fred said he had to order the pan for the Audi and that I'd have to return Monday morning. Meanwhile 3 quarts of oil were added. They even gave me a folded box to place under the hood to absorb the dripping oil.

This morning Fred called bright and early to say that the part had arrived. I went there at 10:30 am. Originally Fred said that someone would drive me home but instead, today, he said it would only take a couple of hours so I explored the nearby area, had a nice lunch across the street at a Vietnamese restaurant. Fred called during lunch saying the car was ready! Talk about efficient service!

Fred and Matthew made what I perceived as an ordeal a lot more easier to handle. Both men are very personable and kind.

Pricewise, I can't compare with others. I was at the point that I just wanted it done asap.
But speaking with people in the know (men, for example-hahaha!) it appears to be reasonable, perhaps even lower than other places.
At the end, there was a lot of handshaking and hugs. Car is purring, and so am I!!!
You will be well-served at Antonio's. Ask for Fred or Matthew.< /Text>

I'm a crawfish lover and whenever I hear of a new crawfish restaurant, I will definitely go to try it.  This is especially true when my friends recommended it and my trust of them makes me eager to go try it. I was very very excited to try this place cuz all of my friends said this place is the best crawfish in town, making me curious. I've ordered Cajun fries, calamari n 6lbs of crawfish; Cajun fries n calamari were good but the crawfish disappointed me, very disappointed. The Cajun sauce wasn't tasty at all and contained lots of oil  üò¨ the meat of the crawfish was very plain as if the seasoning hasn't seeped into the crawfish.  Here is the funny thing, when I looked at the price menu near the cashier I saw that fresh crawfish is $15/lb so I thought that fresh crawfish is available.  I even assured my hb that they will give me the fresh one but when the food came out I can tell those crawfishes weren't 100% fresh but a mixture of both frozen and fresh. My mistake was that I didn't ask them and the waiter didn't let us know first so I could switch to the fresh one because I HATE TO EAT FROZEN CRAWFISH.  Normally when I go to crawfish restaurant and if they serve frozen crawfish they will let the customer know first before they order. Well!  I was right they charged me $11/lb for frozen crawfish.  I hope you guys will make it clear in the future and I think I won't be back again until the taste has improved.</Text>

<review>I couldn't wait to get into my new Mini. Those little cars are so cute and they're made by BMW - must be of good quality, or so I thought.
All the cars come with leather interiors and then there's the option for those sharp looking black enamel spoke wheels.  I ended up getting the Clubman model - it's more spacious than the Cooper and the ride is smoother.  I was happy with my little car ... for about 4 1/2 months, when it needed a brake pad replacement and, as it turned out, a front wheel alignment as well.
Not quite 6 months later, the brake pads needed replacement for the second time .... this is what I have to look forward to ??  I'm so regretful that I didn't go back to Honda - never had problems with those cars.
Honestly, in all my years of driving any make, style, used or new car,  I never had to have the brake pads replaced even once in less than a year.
When I questioned the service manager about the brake pads needing replacement so soon and so frequently, the answer I got was,
"Well, they're a sportier car so the brake pads tend to be a little softer."
Ok ... whatever.
I was also asked:
"Do you drive in a lot of stop and go traffic ?"
Really ??  (this is Los Angeles) Nah, not much.
I'm sorry but brake pads are absolutely essential for the safety of the driver, the passengers and, everyone else on the road.  How does a big name car manufacturer skimp on something as vital as brake pads and be okay with it ??
But if you're really bent on investing in one of those cute little Minis - PLEASE ! buy the extended warranty ... you're gonna need it !<//review>< rate>
1<//rate>

March 4, 2016

On this time of regular check and repair of my BMW X-3
(at BMW of Monrovia, 1425-1451 South Mountain Ave. Monrovia, CA 91016)

This time of regular check was so far good as on the return drive from the service to my house.

But this time repair was very disappointed.
Reason is that both left and right LED rear tail light housings were replaced and charged $792.75 (including labor charge but not including tax).
When I visited at the service for the regular check and the repair, I told and requested the service person to do regular check and to fix only left rear light which was not turned on.
Then, the service person phoned and explained after they checked my X-3 that left rear LED light bulb itself was not be able to be replaced. Instead, whole assemble of rear LED light housings of not only left but also of right should be replaced.
I didn‚Äôt have any choice avoid this expensive and uncomfortable repair charge.

(1)	This time problem is definitely part defects (or parts not reliable). Current technology of LED light bulb is very reliable and long life. And These LED light whole housings are the original ones.  Why should I pay for it?
(2)	This LED housing design was not customer oriented. Because, Customers have to replace whole housing of both left and right instead of left LED light bulb it self. Why BMW (as one of the most honorable automobile manufacturer) had designed such customer uncomfortable one?

If you have any explanation of the reason why or any excuse against my points stated above, please send me an e-mail.
